located on a quiet street in the th district in the west of the city minutes walk from the emblematic Eiffel Tower Champ de Mars and Les Invalides Au Pacific Hotel consists of rooms distributed between two separate buildings surrounding an interior courtyard Rooms with recently renovated en suite bathrooms satellite TV Wi Fi internet connection double glazed windows direct dial telephone and hair dryer Additionally there are family rooms available for up to guests comprising two connecting rooms The hotel also provides hour reception service lift luggage storage safe and internet corner with a computer and printer A typical Paris residential area full of local shops plus Sunday morning street market at Dupleix Thanks to the convenient metro you can reach sights and attractions around the city easily the Champs lys es la Concorde and the Op ra neighbourhood are all less than minutes journey away and the Parc des Expositions trade fair and exhibition centre at the Porte de difference About Amsterdam Highlights Cruise down the historic canals flanked by the city s colourful quaint canal houses some housing the best hotels in Amsterdam wander the cobbled streets of the red light district stopping into wood panelled bars that have been in business for hundreds of years shop the design boutiques and vintage stores of the Streets peruse the rich oil paintings of the Dutch masters at the Rijksmuseum and the Van Gogh Museum step back in time at the poignant Anne Frank House and cycle over the city s brick bridges for a true Amsterdam experience Food Drink Order a plate of buttery Dutch cheeses and wash them down with a local craft beer sample the delicious savoury or sweet crepe pancake hybrid of the pannekoek or snack on a herring sandwich with pickles and onions for a traditional taste of Dutch cuisine Off the Beaten Track Take the free ferry to Amsterdam s up and coming Noord district a former industrial area that s been converted into a sleek new waterside neighbourhood full of re purposed warehouses hosting chic restaurants art galleries and nightclubs Here you can also enjoy the giant green Noorderpark where you can take a yoga or dance class or simply cycle through the park s peaceful paths This is a city that truly has something for everyone starting with our amazing selection of hotels in Amsterdam Choose your favourite and turn Guarantee Relax you ve got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Berlin Highlights Berlin elegant and gritty fashion forward and buttoned up multicoloured and monochrome this city of contrasts is undeniably alive Check out the East Side Gallery s edgy candy coloured murals occupying a kilometre stretch of the former Berlin Wall Brandenburg Gate crowning the entrance to the expansive green Tiergarten park and the Reichstag home of the German Parliament with a gorgeous glass dome with spectacular city views Then there s Potsdamer Platz with its glittering high rises and Sony Centre and on the other end of the architectural spectrum the historic Gendarmenmarkt square flanked by the French and German cathedrals and the stately Konzerthaus theatre For a breath of fresh air the Charlottenburg Palace and gardens are the perfect option before heading back to one of our hotels in Berlin Food Drink Berlin street food is sublime and currywurst is king Chopped up into bite sized morsels this sausage swimming in curry ketchup is a must after hitting up the beer gardens in Hackesche H fe or partying it up in Nollendorfplatz s gay friendly clubs For food with a view try the rooftop restaurant of the Reichstag or the rotating restaurant in Alexanderplatz s TV Tower For a traditional taste there s pork knuckle on sauerkraut washed down with the light and fruity Berliner Weisse beer and for your kaffee und kuchen indulge in a Berliner doughnut Off the Beaten Track The Badeschiff Berlin beach along the Spree River is comprised of a floating turquoise swimming pool a deck where you can practise yoga and sandy riverbanks where you can suntan play beach volleyball or barbecue A cocktail bar and DJ s make this the perfect place to spend summer in the city This is only a tiny taste of everything that awaits in this German gem choose one of our hotels in Berlin and discover everything the city has Guarantee Relax you ve got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Vienna Highlights Regal Vienna is all royal palaces elegant caf s and horse drawn carriages clipping over the cobblestones Make your way to St Stephen s Cathedral where you ll be hypnotised by its kaleidoscopic tiled rooftop and soaring spires which you can climb for a close up Search for Sissi a beloved former Habsburg queen at the sprawling Hofburg Palace and explore the breathtaking Sch nbrunn Palace with its green gardens sprinkled with vibrant blooms Cruise down the Danube River catching glimpses of Vienna s historic cathedrals and its glittering modern towers In the summertime enjoy live music and twinkling lights at the city s canal side caf s and during winter browse the enchanting Christmas market set up in the heart of the old town Whatever you choose to do you ll have the comfort of resting up at one of our hotels in Vienna after your sightseeing Food Drink Chances are once you ve sampled the famous Sachertorte a delectable chocolate cake with apricot jam you ll look for any excuse to duck into one of the city s Art Nouveau coffee houses for a slice with your Viennese coffee For a fortifying meal you can t miss the Wiener Schnitzel a thin cut of veal which is breaded and fried garnished with lemon and parsley and served with chips If you re looking for another alternative to Sachertorte you can always try a warm cinnamony slice of apple strudel it never fails Off the Beaten Track Vienna is the only European capital that actually produces wine within its city limits Try visiting one of the Heurige a name which refers to the wineries serving wine produced that year Gemischter Satz is the most popular made with a whopping total of up to different grape varieties If Austria has awakened your desire to travel don t think twice and have a look at our wonderful hotels in Vienna Browse difference About Florence Highlights The Tuscan treasure of Florence is one of Italy s most storybook cities Start your Italian adventure off with a leisurely breakfast of cappuccino and pastries at one of our hotels in Florence before heading straight to the Piazza del Duomo Here you ll be gobsmacked by the Duomo s marble fa ade of pink cream and olive green hues and giant dome Equally astounding is Michelangelo s David in the Accademia Gallery and the masterpieces by Botticelli da Vinci and Caravaggio at the Uffizi Gallery Rub the snout of the wild boar statue for good luck at the Mercato del Porcellino or shop for souvenirs along the romantic Ponte Vecchio Top it all off by taking in a sunset from the hilltop Piazzale Michelangelo with its achingly beautiful Florence views Food drink Famous for peasant food Florence offers up hearty delights from cannellini bean stew zuppa di fagioli to vegetable and bread stew ribollita and a summer salad with stale bread soaked in tomato juice panzanella Try the famous wild boar with tomato sauce over pappardelle pasta or the mammoth sized bistecca fiorentina best shared between two people For lighter fare head to a wine bar for a glass of Chianti and a tagliere a cutting board with local charcuterie and or cheese Sweet treats include creamy gelato and the scrumptious cantucci an almond biscotti to dip in espresso or dessert wine Finally you ve haven t experienced Florence until you ve sampled its street food lampredotto a cow stomach sandwich that locals love Off the beaten track Getting out of town to visit the Tuscan countryside is a must Wine tasting and food tours are popular options and you can even go truffle hunting in the Tuscan forest for an easy day trip So what are you waiting for Choose your perfect place to stay from our hotels in Florence and you ll be well on your way to your Italian holiday Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in Florence Hotels Cheap Hostels in Florence Guarantee Relax you ve got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference Budget Partner Overview Reviews Map Overview Hotel Beaumarchais little white facade hides a wonderful surprise a modern star establishment situated in the th arrondissement of Paris where you will receive a warm welcome in a relaxed atmosphere The hotel is located in one of the liveliest parts of the city on Rue Oberkampf next to Place de la Republique and near to La Bastille and Le Marais district This area is very central and popular full of bars restaurants and night life where you can easily blend in with the Parisian crowd The hotel has single double twin and triple rooms with a double bed and a single bed in the triples all of which are very modern and tastefully decorated The rooms are equipped with a bathroom with a hair dryer cable TV a telephone wifi Internet connection a safe air conditioning and heating Among the hotel s facilities are a lift a hour reception and a bar cafe Breakfast is served on the pretty green patio not included in the price There is a public car park metres from the hotel Attractive accommodation with the best of Guarantee Relax you ve got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Dublin Highlights From the rich red pub fronts of Temple Bar to pedestrian Grafton Street lined with historic brick buildings and shops to the emerald expanses of St Stephen s Green and Trinity College Dublin is a postcard of a city There are many sights that merit a visit including the ancient Book of Kells in the Trinity College Library the busty statue of Molly Malone and the dapper bronze likeness of James Joyce and the religious sites of Christ Church Cathedral and St Michan s Church complete with a grisly crypt On the flip side Dublin is a city to be experienced Chat up the locals in one of Temple Bar s lively pubs while the band plays Irish folk music catch a Gaelic football game at Croke Park Stadium and picnic in the sprawling Phoenix Park Our hotels in Dublin are nearby all of these top sights but should you ever find yourself in need of directions just ask a friendly Dubliner Food Drink Drinks in Dublin are a no brainer you can pick your poison from beer and whiskey with mandatory visits to the Guinness Storehouse and the Old Jameson Distillery With all the drinking you ll be doing it s a good thing Irish eats are hearty from savoury stews loaded up with tender beef potatoes and veg to fresh fish and chips to piping hot meat pies Don t skip out on dining in a traditional Irish pub it s a quintessential Dublin experience Off the Beaten Track While Ireland calls to mind rolling green hills and dramatic cliffs Dublin is a cosmopolitan city To catch a glimpse of the Irish Sea take a minute journey on the DART to the seaside town of Bray where the Bray Head Cliff Walk winds along the sea cliffs through the green hills for kilometres before finishing up in Greystones Make your way to the Emerald Isle starting by choosing from our amazing hotels in Dublin Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in ll refund you the difference About Rome Highlights Rome the city on seven hills is home to the romantic wreckage of the former Roman empire its ruins lovingly preserved and visited by millions every year If you do nothing else see the Colosseum and the Palatine Hill wandering through the amphitheatre and gardens and lingering over the grass covered remains of the Roman Forum The Baths of Caracalla the soaring dome ceiling of the Pantheon and the recently revamped Trevi Fountain round out the best of Rome s architectural treasures Follow in the footsteps of Audrey Hepburn by savouring a gelato on the Spanish Steps and paying a visit to the Mouth of Truth and don t forget about St Peter s Square and the Sistine Chapel in Vatican City the world s smallest independent state Food Drink Our hotels in Rome are surrounded by some of the city s finest restaurants so you won t have to stray far to sample fresh stuffed pillowy ravioli hand tossed pizza topped with buffalo mozzarella pomodoro tomatoes and basil and creamy parmesan risotto At aperitivo time have a glass of prosecco at a terrace bar and for dessert there s nothing better than a homemade tiramis whipped up from a time worn recipe a scoop of fruity gelato or simply an Italian roasted espresso Off the Beaten Track Gaining ground lately with tourists the authentic Trastevere neighbourhood has everything that makes Rome great Ivy covered trattorias illuminated at night with strands of twinkling lights cobblestone streets with tucked away artisan workshops and the Gianicolo Hill begging to be scaled for postcard views of Rome trust us it s worth the walk Have a look at our hotels in Rome and find the perfect place to stay for your Roman holiday Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in Rome refund you the difference About London London is quite simply the place to be the UK capital is one of the coolest most dynamic and cosmopolitan cities on the planet with a virtually endless array of attractions for all tastes and ages As the saying goes when a man is tired of London he is tired of life Highlights Watch the changing of the guard at Buckingham Palace see ancient treasures from around the globe in the British Museum shop until you drop on Oxford Street and take in the view from way up high on the London Eye In the evening check out the city s famous nightlife in trendy Soho and Camden or catch a West End show before heading back to one of our hotels in London Food Drink The infamous fish and chips are a must while in London and there s nothing better than tucking into a steaming shepherd s pie on a rainy London day Savour the city s international flavours by going in for dumplings in Chinatown or trying out a creamy curry at one of London s many traditional Indian restaurants Off the Beaten Track Travelling with kids Take them to the Hackney City Farm just above Shoreditch where they can pet the animals and you can partake in a farm fresh brunch For an alternative bird s eye view to the London Eye try the Emirates Air Line Cable Car across the Thames from the Royal Docks to The O Arena Are you packing your bags yet Reserve one of our hotels in Highlights Lisbon Portugal s beautiful capital overlooks the River Tagus as it empties into the Atlantic Ocean The city undulates steeply over several hills and is crowned by the castle of S o Jorge which offers spectacular views The Bairro Alto and Alfama two of Lisbon s oldest and most enchanting neighbourhoods are home to Fado houses bars and restaurants while the Baixa district and the elegant Avenida da Liberdade are the best areas for shopping Just of the original elevadores or funiculars built to link the upper with the lower neighbourhoods survive and have become like the nostalgic no tram a popular tourist attraction Try the Elevador Santa Justa for a magnificent bird s eye view over the city s rooftops and Tagus River before heading back to one of our hotels in Lisbon to rest and relax Food drink A wonderful destination for foodies the dining scene in Lisbon offers plenty of award winning restaurants and fashionable bistros but its greatest strength is the old fashioned traditional restaurant offering the fantastic local produce Fresh fish and shellfish features prominently on many menus along with classic dishes such as caldo verde kale soup flavoured with chorizo Lisbon is justly famous for its excellent bread and local pastries which include the famous pasteis de nata tiny custard tarts dusted with cinnamon Off the beaten track Gra a is a charming historic district in the heart of Lisbon which hasn t yet made it on to the tourist radar It has several miradors viewing points from where you can admire the sunset or enjoy a picnic and the area also has some wonderful arty caf s and bars This wonderful European capital is the perfect place for a city break so have a look at our fantastic hotels in Lisbon and start planning your trip About Paris Highlights This entrancing city straddling the River Seine has more than years of history embodied in spectacular buildings such as the Notre Dame Cathedral a jewel of Gothic architecture with its guardian gargoyles Paying a visit to the Mona Lisa at her home in the Louvre is a must as is spending some time with the impressionists in the luminous converted railway station the lovely Mus e d Orsay Shop the boho chic boutiques of Montmartre or the swanky designer stores on the Champs lys es and cap it all off with an evening ascent of the Eiffel Tower before heading home to one of our cosy hotels in Paris Food Drink Breakfast on croissants and caf au lait experience the pageantry of French nouvelle cuisine in one of Paris many Michelin starred restaurants or dig into comfort foods like cassoulet with crusty French bread and a glass of Bordeaux in a traditional brasserie C est magnifique Off the Beaten Track Stroll through the tranquil tree filled P re Lachaise Cemetery where you can visit the tombs of Jim Morrison Edith Piaf and Oscar Wilde among others or check out the Frank Gehry designed Fondation Louis Vuitton that houses incredible contemporary art and hosts cultural events in the pretty Bois de Boulogne park Whether you re a seasoned Paris vet or a newbie itching to get to the city of lights for the first time the best way to start off your trip is by checking out our stellar hotels in Paris Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in Paris Hotels Cheap Hostels in Paris Hostels Cheap Apartments in Paris Apartments Cheap B Bs in Paris B Bs Map Overview This basic star hotel in Paris is conveniently situated in the th arrondissement just a short walk away from the Canal Saint Martin and the rue Oberkampf famous for its nightlife The Luna Park Hotel offers simple rooms with a private or shared bathroom all with a TV telephone and Wi Fi The hotel also has a hour reception service a TV lounge a left luggage office and a safe The hotel is located near the Place de la Bastille in a vibrant area of Paris full of bars and caf s The famous P re Lachaise cemetery where Jim Morrison is buried is just a minute walk away You can pick up metro services at the Place de la R publique minutes away on foot to top sights across the city get to the Louvre in minutes Invalides and the Eiffel Tower in minutes and the Gare du Nord in just minutes Highlights It s impossible not to fall in love with Prague With its gingerbread house architecture scattered around cobblestone squares this Czech city will give you an eyeful of stunning sights Start off by crossing Charles Bridge where you ll wander by artists hawking their wares and watercolours as you cross the Vltava River Up on Golden Lane you ll find colourful houses littered along this alleged alchemists alley one of which where writer Franz Kafka once resided From here you re perfectly poised to visit the medieval Prague Castle and the Gothic style St Vitus Cathedral which will keep you occupied for the better part of a day After you ve soaked up the views on castle hill head to the Old Town Square where you can marvel over the magical Prague Astronomical Clock with its golden gears and appreciate Czech art at its finest in the Prague National Gallery A cruise down the Vltava makes a perfect evening activity before heading back to one of our hotels in Prague for a well deserved rest Food Drink Packing a punch of flavours Czech goulash is slow food at its finest This rich stew incorporates tender braised beef and veggies with a side of Prague s famous bread dumplings Pair it with a Pilsner Prague s local beer and you ve got the makings of a fantastic meal Don t miss the savoury street food found at sausage stands where you can pick up a sauerkraut topped brat If you ve got a sweet tooth make sure to sample trdelnik a curly cue of a pastry sprinkled with sugar Off the Beaten Track David ern s offbeat art can be found throughout Prague most notably his climbing alien baby sculptures on the i kov TV Tower ern s creations stick out in classical Prague so make sure to go hunting for all of his offbeat gems This storybook city is a must on any traveller s list so have a look at our hotels in Prague and plan your next getaway Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in Prague Hotels Cheap Hostels in Prague Hostels Cheap Apartments in Prague below Credit card guarantee Our collaborating establishments require the user s credit card details in order to secure the reservation This information is supplied directly to the establishment where the reservation has been made When making a reservation the client directly accepts an agreement with the establishment chosen EnGrande will directly charge the client s credit card a prepayment which corresponds to a part of or the total cost of the reservation This online payment is made in EUROS other currencies may be shown for your information only and may vary according to the exchange rates When this has been completed it means that the reservation has been confirmed and the establishment availability will be blocked for the dates of your reservation The remaining amount of the total charge will be paid in local currency directly upon your arrival at the establishment unless otherwise indicated You can book for up to people at a single establishment and for a maximum of nights We have Secure Sockets Layer SSL software from DigiCert which guarantees encryption of credit card data sent via the Internet preventing third party access to this information This software ensures that every transaction is secure Pre authorisations Some hotels have a policy to carry out pre authorisations of the credit card to confirm the reservation They may do it before the client s date of arrival in order to check that the card is still valid and to verify that there is enough credit to cover the cost of the reservation If the card is not valid or does not have enough credit to cover the amount due to be paid on arrival we urge the client to get in contact with the accommodation and provide details of a valid card If there is an error during the pre authorisation process the hotel may cancel the reservation It is therefore very important that the client makes sure the credit card used during the reservation process is valid and has enough credit until the day of arrival to avoid the reservation being cancelled Should the hotel cancel the booking please note that the cancellation policy of your reservation will apply BudgetPartner non refundable rate conditions The establishment will charge the full remaining balance in local currency at any time after booking If the credit card used to make the booking is invalid or has insufficient funds the hotelier will cancel the reservation and the amount paid online will not be refunded A BudgetPartner establishment is an establishment that has been directly contracted by EnGrande and is indicated with the BudgetPartner logo PayPal payment conditions The customer must make sure that the billing agreement with us remains active until the check out date has passed to avoid the cancellation of their reservation Should the reservation be cancelled please note that the cancellation policy of your reservation will apply Fully prepaid rate conditions The customer will be charged the total amount by credit card at the time of making the online reservation This amount will be always charged in EUROS other currencies may be shown for your information only and may vary according to the current exchange rate Please note that if you pay in other currencies you may be charged transaction fees by your bank Cancellations and no show policy BudgetPartner establishments A BudgetPartner is an price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Venice Highlights Navigating the cobbled streets canals and bridges of this romantic floating city feels like stepping back in time a sensation that is magnified as you wander the grand hallways of the Doge s Palace in St Mark s Square from its perch on the Grand Canal Take the lift to the top of the bell tower in Saint Mark s Basilica for a bird s eye view snap a pic with Venice s famous pigeons go on a gondola ride under the Bridge of Sighs and feel like a verified Venetian channel your inner fashionista by shopping the designer Italian brands on the Calle Larga XXII Marzo and explore the oil paintings of Italian masters at the Accademia Gallery Food Drink Whet your appetite with a few cicchetti Venetian canap s and a bellini at the place of its invention Harry s Bar before savouring seafood based delicacies like risotto al nero a rice dish made with squid ink polenta e schie a creamy cornmeal porridge with small shrimp and bigoli a whole wheat pasta served with meat or seafood ragout Cap it all off by savouring a gelato while strolling through Venice s winding streets perfection Off the Beaten Track Many a tourist makes it to the island of Murano where the famous glass blowers practice their craft but the nearby Burano island sees less tourist traffic and is refund you the difference About Madrid Highlights There is an old school elegance to Madrid and you can see it as you wander along the tree lined Paseo del Prado stroll through the upscale Salamanca neighbourhood with its Retiro Park oasis savour a strong cup of Spanish coffee in the Plaza Mayor and explore the glittering business district crowned by the enormous leaning Kio Towers a stone s throw from the famous Santiago Bernabeu football stadium Madrid s Golden Triangle of art museums formed by the Prado Thyssen Bornemisza and Reina Sofia are fully worth wandering through to gaze upon famous works by Goya Picasso and Vel zquez Follow in the footsteps of royalty at the Palacio Real and explore the varied wares at the famous Sunday Rastro Market before heading back to one of our hotels in Madrid for some much needed rest Food Drink Madrile os love their meat and above all ham is king In many a bar you ll be greeted by the sight of hundreds of hams hanging from the ceiling waiting to be thinly sliced and served up solo Check out the tapas bars in the central Plaza de Santa Ana or along the posh Calle de Ponzano or dig into a traditional bocadillo de calamares a submarine sandwich filled with fried squid rings and sip a glass of sangria or tinto de verano If you re visiting when the weather turns chilly there s nothing better than tucking in to a steaming bowl of cocido madrile o a stew made with chickpeas and tender beef and sausage Off the Beaten Track Everyone knows the museums of the Golden Triangle but the lesser known cultural centres of El Matadero and La Tabacalera offer an awesome glimpse of alternative art while the intimate garden and home of the Museo Sorolla offers up the masterpieces of the artist s dreamy beach scenes For a peek into the past try visiting And n or the ghost platform to see a perfectly preserved s metro station The only piece left in the puzzle is to choose one of our hotels in Madrid and your Spanish holiday Highlights New York City the Big Apple the city that never sleeps and immortalised in Frank Sinatra s famous song in a single day you could take an early morning stroll across the Brooklyn Bridge shop Soho picnic in Central Park see the sun set from the top of the Empire State Building and top it all off with an evening Broadway show Museum hop to your heart s content from the MoMA to the American Museum of Natural History wander through the lofty New York Public Library and Grand Central Station catch a Yankees or a Knicks game and ride on the Ferris wheel on Coney Islands beachside boardwalk The best part All of our hotels in New York are right in the heart of the action Food Drink The New York City food scene is a smorgasbord of every imaginable style and ingredient under the sun You ll have to work up an appetite to fit in all of the city s standbys starting with a cheesy slice of New York pizza from Joe s a Gray s Papaya hot dog smothered in ketchup mustard and caramelised onions a triple decker pastrami sandwich from Carnegie Deli chicken and waffles for a taste of soul food in Harlem and Peking duck and dumplings in Chinatown Save room for dessert because it would be a sin not to try a cannoli from Ferrara Bakery in Little Italy and a slice of Junior s New York cheesecake in Brooklyn Don t worry you ll be doing lots of walking Off the Beaten Track The New York High Line completed in is a mile long park spanning the Meatpacking District and Chelsea overtop the former railroad tracks of what was once the West Side Line Now you can stroll along the train tracks full of flowers greenery and park benches and enjoy views of the Hudson River and the city Everyone is dying to take this trip and choosing one of our hotels in New York is the first step to turning your dream vacation into a reality Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in New York Hotels Cheap Hostels in New York Hostels Cheap Apartments in New York Apartments Cheap B Bs in New York B Bs Reviews Map Overview With Wi Fi and a c this inviting hotel enjoys a fantastic location in the elegant Op ra neighbourhood of central Paris a minute walk from the upmarket department stores along the Grands Boulevards as well as Louvre and the Champs lys es Each of the rooms at the star Hotel London offers a private bathroom some with whirlpool baths as well as a TV air conditioning and Wi Fi A continental breakfast is available if required and the hotel also offers a hour reception and a lift from reception only please note that there is a flight of stairs from street level to the reception The hotel enjoys a perfect location in the heart of Paris within easy walking distance of a host of top attractions whether you want to stroll down the Champs lys es visit the glorious th century opera house or admire the world class art collections at the Louvre budgetplaces guest rating out of based on reviews TripAdvisor traveller rating based on reviews TripAdvisor LLC See map Favourite search Clear all filters remove Establishment type Hotel Hostel Apartment Bed and breakfast Cheap Hotels near Gare de Lyon Paris The Gare de Lyon is the third largest rail terminal in Paris in terms of passenger and traffic volume Metro RER TGV and other regional and national routes are all available at this beautiful station located in the upbeat th district of Paris where by the way you can choose from a range of cheap hotels apartments and other types of budget accommodation The Gare de Lyon is visible in the distance thanks to the huge clock tower which tells passengers the time from the four cardinal points If you want to stay close to one of the main transport hubs in Paris check out our range of cheap hotels and apartments close to Gare de Lyon Other sights and neighbourhoods boutiques shops and cinemas the Champs Elys es is without a doubt the most iconic avenue in Paris Although there are hardly any hotels in Paris not to mention B Bs located on the Champs Elys es itself its length and location mean it s easily reached wherever your stay The avenue runs between two major Paris squares Place Charles de Gaulle where the Arc de Triomphe is found and Place de la Concorde home to the Luxor Obelisk If you re in Paris for any major celebration the chances are you ll end up heading to the Champs Elys es This is particularly true for Christmas and New Year s when the avenue is beautifully lit up and for the famous parade on Bastille Day Our cheap accommodation in Paris in the centre of Paris means you can enjoy all the action on the Champs Elys es at bargain got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Brussels Highlights Polished Brussels exudes elegances from each of its quaint caf s cobblestone squares and charming churches The city s mascot its cheeky little statue the Manneken Pis gets dressed up in whimsical costumes ranging from Elvis to Nelson Mandela and everything in between Just steps away is Brussels Grand Place the buzzing central square the rest of the city swirls around Here you ll be surrounded by opulent buildings bedecked in gold trim and the marvellous Flower Carpet in August An art lover s paradise the Sablon neighbourhood contains the Royal Museum of Fine Arts the Centre for Fine Arts and the Magritte Museum the surrealist son of Belgium The young and the young at heart will love the Brussels Comic Book Museum as well as the awesome Atomium a gigantic model of an atom housing various exhibitions and the Mini Europe Park where you can wander by models of Europe s top architectural gems Finally don t forget to check out the European Union buildings glittering edifices on the edge of the Jubelpark before heading back to one of our hotels in Brussels Food Drink Belgium is famous for its beer and chocolate both of which are on offer in Brussels When you need to wet your whistle you can sip on Saisons Belgian blondes and fruity lambics Every beer has its own distinctive glass so order at random for the most variety Belgium s coveted chocolates are legendary and in Brussels you can pick up these blissful blends at Neuhaus Fr d ric Blondeel Godiva and Leonidas among countless others Finally if you re feeling peckish pick up some frites on the go preferably smothered in andalouse a sauce of tomato paste mayonnaise and peppers filters remove Establishment type Hotel Hostel Apartment Bed and breakfast Cheap Hotels in Montmartre Paris What to see With its cobbled streets and charmingly old fashioned architecture the hilltop neighbourhood of Montmartre is one of the most appealing in Paris and has been popularised in films like Am lie A century ago this bohemian district was a crucible for some of the most important artistic and intellectual movements of the th century and remains a popular area for artists Remnants of its old atmosphere survive in cabarets such as the Moulin Rouge now much sanitised but still hugely popular The neighbourhood is crowned by the Basilica of Sacr Coeur one of Paris most recognisable landmarks there are stunning views over the city from the square in front of the church Local vibe Montmartre is a very popular tourist destination its streets and squares always packed by day or night It s full of usually pricy shops caf s and bars walk a little further afield to find more reasonably priced options Practicalities The most convenient metro stations for Montmartre are Abbesses Barb s Rochechouart Anvers Ch teau Rouge and Lamarck Caulaincourt It s also served by a funicular which operates from near the Place Suzanne Valadon at the bottom of the hill and the basilica at the top Check out our great range of cheap hotels in Montmartre Paris Other sights and neighbourhoods in Paris th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th arrondissement th Both cosmopolitan and charming there s a little something for everyone here It s impossible not to be awed by Milan s wedding cake of a Duomo and you can explore the terraces to see its spires up close and get a great view of the bustling Piazza del Duomo Just next door you ll find the Galleria Vittorio Emanuele II housing designer shops amidst skylights and frescoes Continuing on you ll find the Piazza della Scala crowned by a statue of Italian legend Leonardo da Vinci plus the Teatro Alla Scala with its sumptuous crimson and gold interiors and top notch Italian operas See Da Vinci s masterpiece The Last Supper at the pinky hued Santa Maria delle Grazie Basilica and then spend an afternoon wandering through the lush Sempione Park Exploring Italy is quite a feat so make sure you allot time for resting relaxing and cocktails at one of our incredible hotels in Milan Food Drink Mouth watering Milanese cuisine is as much a feast for your eyes as it is for your taste buds Try risotto alla Milanese vibrant yellow with saffron and plenty of butter and Parmesan Carnivores will love the crispy cotoletta alla Milanese veal breaded and saut ed in butter which could be accompanied by the creamy polenta Milan is famous for Vegetarians will adore hearty minestrone a vegetable soup perfect for chilly days but also served cold in summer And whatever you do don t forget to save room for gelato Off the Beaten Track Did you know Milan has its own network of canals The area known as Navigli is the perfect place to sip an Aperol spritz or a glass of Prosecco as you nibble tasty aperitivo canal side All of this and more make Italy s fashion capital a must see so check out our hotels in Milan and cross this city off your travel bucket list Browse establishments by got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Stockholm Highlights Made up of islands Stockholm begs to be explored Start with Gamla Stan the charming old town where you ll find the Royal Palace and the Stockholm Cathedral with its lifelike statue of Saint George slaying the dragon After you ve wandered the cobbled tree lined streets with their pastel gingerbread houses and hotels hop a boat to the magnificent Drottningholm Palace another of Sweden s royal residences akin to Versailles To complete the royal tour Djurg rden island is a must think former royal hunting grounds converted into a breathtaking park Here you ll find the Rosendal summer palace the famous Vasamuseet ship museum the Skansen open air history museum the kitschy Abba Museum plus tons of waterfront biking and walking trails For an alternative option head to S dermalm Stockholm s largest island and home to hipster caf s boutiques bars and art galleries Take your pick of our hotels in Stockholm on the island that best suits your travel personality Food Drink Swedish meatballs are a Stockholm classic served with a savoury sauce and vibrant fuchsia lingonberries Street food is a popular budget option from hot dogs with crazy toppings like mashed potatoes and shrimp salad to herring burgers If you re really starving you can t go wrong with a smorgasbord a buffet containing traditional dishes made with herring and shrimp smoked salmon crisp Swedish flat bread and sides like potatoes with sour cream and dill Off the Beaten Track Stockholm summers are the best and there s no better place to enjoy a sunny day on the archipelago than the Fj derholmarna islands Cruise to the main island a grassy tree filled knoll perfect for spreading out a towel and sunbathing or visit the brewery where you can sip craft beers overlooking the marina If a northern European island holiday sounds like your style check out our hotels in Stockholm and start planning your trip Browse establishments by category Cheap Hotels in Stockholm Hotels Cheap Hostels in Stockholm Hostels Cheap Apartments in Stockholm Apartments Cheap B Bs in contains Columbus tomb to the lavish Royal Palace Take a stroll through the enchanting Barrio Santa Cruz its whitewashed houses trimmed with flower filled balconies and home to some of the most beautiful boutique hotels in Seville or cool off amid the palm trees and colourfully tiled fountains of the Parque Maria Luisa Food and Drink Seville offers some of the best and most varied tapas in Spain with myriad bars and restaurants providing everything from platters of Iberian ham to the latest gourmet creations Gazpacho a chilled tomato soup is a local favourite along with freshly cooked pescaito frito small fried fish A glass of fino or manzanilla sherry served very cold makes a refreshing ap ritif Off the Beaten Track Seville is full of hidden corners such as the wonderful secret garden at the Casa de Pilatos with its intricate tiles and blazing bougainvillea Relax at one of the terrace caf s on the Alameda de Hercules or visit the art collection in the th century Hospital de los Venerables Be enchanted by our hotels in Seville where the air is filled with the scent of jasmine and flamenco rhythms float above the sinuous streets secret gardens and tinkling fountains Browse got the best price possible If you see the same offer for less on another website we ll refund you the difference About Barcelona Highlights Perhaps the most stylish city on the Mediterranean Barcelona has an enchanting medieval heart magnificent Modernista mansions and of course several kilometres of gorgeous beaches Crowned by the Sagrada Fam lia Gaud s enormous and as yet unfinished masterpiece the city s outstanding architecture is rivalled by its fantastic shops bars clubs and restaurants Stroll along the Rambla choose picnic ingredients at the Boqueria Market get lost in the narrow lanes of the Gothic Quarter or simply dance until dawn at a beachfront club before heading back to one of our gorgeous hotels in Barcelona Food drink Barcelona is world famous as a destination for gourmets and is home to some of the finest restaurants in Spain Whether you re looking for the latest hotspot serving molecular gastronomy or just want some patates braves and a cold beer by the beach Barcelona has something for everyone Catalan staples which you ll find in traditional eateries across town include pa amb tom quet thick slices of bread rubbed with tomato garlic and olive oil fideu similar to paella but made with small noodles butifarra amb mongetes pork sausage cooked with white beans and escalivada slivers of roast peppers and aubergine Off the beaten track Barcelona has scores of wonderful parks where you can escape the crowds with a picnic several are located on the hill of Montju c which enjoys panoramic views over the whole city and you can even find quiet corners of the Park G ell if you keep heading uphill The Horta Labyrinth a beautiful park with an th century maze at its heart is Barcelona s most romantic park and the Parc de Collserola which spreads across the hills behind the city offers great hikes and mountain bike trails Have a look at our wonderful list of hotels in Barcelona and start planning your trip today Browse establishments by category
